Nous espérons que vous allez bien.

Votre participation est essentielle pour nous permettre de créer un outil utile et efficace. Vos retours nous aideront à comprendre les fonctionnalités et les services que vous attendez d'un chatbot scolaire.

For expired domains, you have a renewal grace period of up to 30 days (depending on your domain extension), during which you can reactivate at the regular rate. After that, however, your domain will be placed in redemption and you’ll need to contact our Support Team if you wish to recover it. Welcome to this week’s edition of the LlamaIndex newsletter! We’re bringing you an exciting set of updates and valuable resources from Mixture-of-Agents (MoA) paper as LlamaPack to how AtomicWork’s Atom AI assistant leverages LlamaIndex to boost productivity and manage data effectively. Be sure to check out our in-depth guides, educational tutorials, and webinars for deeper insights into our tools.

We’re introducing new terms on the use of Miro AI features

On July 17, 2024, we’re introducing a new AI Features Addendum <https://click.e.miro.com/?qs=51ff0f79a76ea9c07f5d21ff7724896ae8ef33bcf3bc5fe4e35f087d0fcc5e6123f21aaba6836133aa1f2ead9a6b14fffd824dc0bfb918504ae07758974a345d>  that will supplement the agreement you have with Miro. We’re also updating the Miro Privacy Policy <https://click.e.miro.com/?qs=51ff0f79a76ea9c02297f89ac6c6498e5bd3d61bef35c23357f1ec97f8e2479bd2a2a0061c51bc53e75e072ad26ecb0430f21f1d902ee5021270bac0a75e0556> . These changes make it easier for you to understand what to expect from Miro as you use our AI features, such as Miro Assist.

	
You can review the new terms here <https://click.e.miro.com/?qs=51ff0f79a76ea9c07f5d21ff7724896ae8ef33bcf3bc5fe4e35f087d0fcc5e6123f21aaba6836133aa1f2ead9a6b14fffd824dc0bfb918504ae07758974a345d> . At a glance, these updates explain:

•	 How Miro uses inputs you provide and output generated by Miro AI features.

•	 Ownership of output generated by Miro’s AI features.

•	 Limitations associated with the quickly-evolving technologies that underpin Miro AI features.

	
You don't have to do anything to accept these changes. By continuing to use Miro after July 17th you are agreeing to the new terms. If you have questions check the FAQ below.

	

AI Features Addendum FAQ

We don’t train generative AI with your board content. Miro relies on commercially available models (such as developed by OpenAI) as well as open-source models that are trained with licensed data and public domain content where copyright has expired. Miro may use usage data and other meta data to improve your product experience and develop features like diagramming and sticky clustering.

	
You can choose not to participate in our AI feature improvement efforts. We currently don’t use your input into and output from Miro AI features to improve our product. If we intend to change our training approach, we will inform you upfront.

	
You own your board content. No license granted to Miro to operate its services will supersede your ownership rights.

	
Thank you for using Miro! 
The Miro Team

Hi Marwane,

The internet is broken. It’s flooded with ads, spam, misinformation, disinformation, division, and hate.

At Medium, we say our purpose is to “deepen your understanding of the world.”

If you're like us, if you're curious, if you're hungry to deepen your understanding of your world, if you think we can do better than the current standard of how the internet works, then now is an important time to invest in yourself and us.

Imagine a place that:

*	Respects your time, free from ads and spam
*	Recommends the most informed writers, not the loudest
*	Protects you from a deluge of spam, fraud, and AI-generated content
*	Promotes deeper understanding, not misunderstanding or division
*	Rewards writers to do even more of the hard work of researching and articulating their ideas and knowledge.

That's Medium. Our members are helping us build it. Won't you join us?

Be part of a better internet.
– The team at Medium
